<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>
<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>
<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>

<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>
<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>
<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>

<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>
<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>
<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>

<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>
<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>
<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>

<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>

<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>

<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>

<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>
<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>

<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>

<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>

<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>
<s> own drinking also 6 lenghth of old junk [8 2 att 6 am <\s>

<s> know where he was <\s>

<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>

<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
<s> of clarett and some sugar and a quarter cask for the capts <\s>

<s> left the poor frenchman in hopes of letting his capt <\s>
<s> know where he was <\s>
<s> weighd anchor from the mold for cape maze with a fresh gale att nw <\s>
<s> gillmore our mate resignd his birth not being qualifyed for it <\s>
<s> john webb was put in his room <\s>
<s> footnote 82 old rope _thursday 24 att 1 pm <\s>
<s> jennings also a pistoll to james hayes with whom the capt <\s>
<s> exchanged a muskett for a fowling peice he had <\s>
<s> _wednesday 9th squally weather with rain <\s>
<s> lett humphry walters and tim'y northwood have 5 yds <\s>
<s> of ozenbrig each for frock and trowsers also 6 yds <\s>
<s> markt the sloops arms on the butt with letter r and the pistolls with a cross on the stock <\s>
<s> _thursday 10th opened a bb <\s>
<s> _friday 11th the first settled day since we left providence <\s>
<s> the joyners made an arm chest to carry in the pinnace when we go on the look out <\s>
<s> lattitude per mas'rs obs'n 24:32 <\s>
<s> _saturday 12 fresh breezes of wind with some squalls of rain <\s>
<s> saw the land off the poup <\s>
<s> it was the crocassess 71 footnote 71 caicos probably rocky islets at the southeast of the bahama group _sunday 13th the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a case bottle of rum for a tropick bottle 72 for his pinnace <\s>
<s> the people chrisned her and named her the _spaniards dread <\s>
<s> made the land of hispaniola and the island of tortudas 73 we have now gott in cruizing ground the lord send us good success against our ennemies <\s>
<s> squally rainy weather for the most part of these 24 hours <\s>
<s> footnote 72 a bottle with which to celebrate the crossing of the line of the tropic of cancer footnote 73 tortuga north of haiti _munday 14th hard gales of wind <\s>
<s> brought too off of trotudas under our foresail <\s>
<s> saw a sloop bearing down upon us <\s>
<s> gott all things ready to receive her <\s>
<s> fired our bow chase then hoisted our jibb and main sail and gave her chase and we out sailing of her she brot <\s>
<s> she was a sloop from philadelphia bound to jamaica <\s>
<s> too again under our ballast main it blowing a meer frett of wind att no <\s>
<s> of beef and a tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _tuesday 15 still under ballast-main sail <\s>
<s> loost our fore sail and took the reef out of our main sail <\s>
<s> saw the land which proved to be cape maze 74 footnote 74 cape maysi the eastern point of cuba _wednesday 16 moderate weather but an uncommon wind att so <\s>
<s> cruzing off of cape maze <\s>
<s> nixon a new hand a gun and cartouch box to marshall a pistoll and cartouch box he having lost his that he had found him before to ephraim read and benjn <\s>
<s> blanchard each a pistoll theirs being broke and to humphry walters a cutlasses having lost is his given him before all which arms they are to pay for <\s>
<s> _thursday 17 still cruizing as above <\s>
<s> saw 2 sloops one on our starbord and the other on the larboard bow steering no west <\s>
<s> we fired severall shott to bring them too but one of them was obstinate <\s>
<s> too att the first shott <\s>
<s> he was come from jamaica and bound to york <\s>
<s> he informd us that there was a large fleet just arrived from england to join the admiral that admiral vernon was gone to st <\s>
<s> aga 75 de cuba that there was a hott press both by sea and land and that the spanish admiral with a large man of warr was blown up att the avanah 76 which news we hope is true that the other sloop was one capt <\s>
<s> styles bound also to york and saild in comp'y with him that there was a ship also to load 76a which we saw with a schooner the former bound to london and the schooner to rhode island <\s>
<s> styles received some damage by his obstinacy for not bringing too having hulled him and tore his sails <\s>
<s> saw a top sail vessell the master going to mast-head to see what course she steer'd had the misfortune to break his arm just above his wrist <\s>
<s> gave the vessell chase as farr as inagua island 77 where she brot <\s>
<s> we made the capt <\s>
<s> come on board with his papers <\s>
<s> he came from lougan 78 and was bound to nantz in france loaded with sugar indigo and hydes also 300 ps <\s>
<s> of 8/ 8 sent by the intendant to the receiver of the customs of nantz <\s>
<s> we went aboard in his yawl and found his cargo agreeable to his bills of lading and manifest togather with his clearance so lett him past <\s>
<s> he informed us that there was a brigt <\s>
<s> belonging to the spaniards att lougan that came in there by disstress having lost his mast which gentleman we hope to have the honour to dine or sup with before long <\s>
<s> he further told us that the last north wind had done great damage having drove severall vessell to sea all unrigged <\s>
<s> vernon and wentworth having failed to take cartagena were now planning an attack which proved to be equally unsuccessful on santiago de cuba footnote 76 the _invencible_ flagship of don rodrigo de torres was struck by lightning in havana harbor june 30 1741 and blown up <\s>
<s> letter of the viceroy horcasitas that day describing the occurrence in pezuela _historia de cuba ii <\s>
<s> the admiral did not perish footnote 76a leeward footnote 77 a large island in the southern bahamas footnote 78 léogane in haiti french _friday 18th calm weather for these 24 hours <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> saw two sails under cape nicholas 79 but coud not speak with them it being start [8 0 calm <\s>
<s> the mas'r is in a fair way of doing well with his arm <\s>
<s> footnote 79 the northwest cape of haiti footnote 80 stark _saturday 19th still moderate weather <\s>
<s> _sunday 20th att 5 pm <\s>
<s> came up with the chase <\s>
<s> she proved to be a french ship that was blown out of loogan in the hurricane 6 days ago <\s>
<s> she was obliged to cut her mizenmast to gett clear of the land <\s>
<s> her quarters were all stove in and her head carried away and neither anchor nor cable aboard but perrishing for want of water <\s>
<s> she had 16 hands aboard and but one sailor which was the master <\s>
<s> she had on board 30 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar one hhd <\s>
<s> and a barrell of indigo 13 hhds <\s>
<s> of bourdeaux wine and provisions plenty <\s>
<s> we ordered his boat on board <\s>
<s> as soon as the master came over the side he fell on his knees and beg'd for help and told us his deplorable case <\s>
<s> we spared him some water and put one of our hands aboard to navigate his vessell he being an intire stranger on the coast <\s>
<s> he kept comp'y with us all night <\s>
<s> the mas'r sent us a hhd <\s>
<s> saw the ship a league to windward of us <\s>
<s> we then made in for the mole by cape nicholas [8 1 and she steering after us we bro't her in but the wind coming ahead and his ship out of trim coud not work up as far as we so she came to an anchor a league below us <\s>
<s> of the ship is named doulteau the ship _la genereuse from rochell in france dutch built <\s>
<s> pork and a bb <\s>
<s> footnote 81 the mole which gives the port its present name of mole-saint-nicolas _munday 21st our lieut <\s>
<s> went ashoare to see if he coud kill any cattle with 2 more hands <\s>
<s> some of the people went to find water found 7 wells cleared them <\s>
<s> the people on board being in fishing cought abundance of fish <\s>
<s> some of our hands compl ained they were poisoin'd by eating of the fish <\s>
<s> our pinnace went to the ship to tow her up but the sea breeze coming in fresh was obliged to moor her as well as we cou'd <\s>
<s> _tuesday 22d the capt <\s>
<s> sent me a board the ship to know if they wanted any assistance <\s>
<s> they fired a gun and hoisted a light for the pinnace to come on board to tow them up <\s>
<s> sent her with 20 hands and towd her above where we lay and moor'd her head and stern free from all dangers <\s>
<s> our people very busy in wooding and watering <\s>
<s> _wednesday 23 att 6 pm <\s>
<s> the master of the ship chas <\s>
<s> tesier came on board to return our capt <\s>
<s> thanks for his kind assistance and offered him any thing he might have occasion for <\s>
<s> he gave the people another hhd <\s>
